<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stamcel.html>stamcel</a> (112731)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stam.html>stam</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cel.html>cel</a></i>, calque <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a>  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Stammzelle</i>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:starling.html>starling</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:sterling.html>sterling</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">sterlinge</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">starlinc</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">stærlinc</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:starling.html>starling</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">stær</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:starling.html>starling</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">-linc, -ling</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos"><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
